# ::edge	everything	op1	generous-41	0.1	0	
# ::edge	generous-41	ARG1	so	0	0.0	
(g / generous-41 
      :ARG1 (s / so) 
      :op-of (e / everything) 
      :op-of (a / and))

      :ARG0 (w / whole) 
      :ARG1 (q / quantity) 
      :op-of (y / yet 
            :op1 (l / less)))

(g / generous-41 
      :ARG0 (t / they) 
      :ARG1 (o / once) 
      :time-of (f / famous 
            :domain (t2 / they 
                  :domain-of (r / rich)) 
            :op-of (a / and)))
